 Union Minister of State for Home Affairs G
 Kishan Reddy said in written reply to a question related to crimes against women in the Lok Sabha that the safety of women is the first priority of the government
 unhone kaha ki iske liye sarkaar ne puure desh main tamaam tarah kii pahal kii he
 Enumerating the measures taken by the government for women's safety, he said that the Criminal Law (amendment) Act, 2013 was enacted to give effect to the law against sexual offenses and to prevent crimes
 iske baad, aapraadhik kanoon (sanshodhan) adhinium, 2018 laayaa gaya
 Under this, more stringent punitive provisions were enacted, including capital punishment for raping a girl under 12 years of age

 iske tahat sankat ke samay ghatnasthal kii pahchaan kii bhicomputerikrutvyavastha he
